          (bn1): BatchNorm2d(8, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
          (conv2): Conv2d(8, 64, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn2): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (avgpool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
  (fc): PAIModulePyThread(
    (layerArray): ModuleList(
      (0-3): 4 x Linear(in_features=64, out_features=1000, bias=True)
    )
  )
)

      (layerArray): ModuleList(
        (0-3): 4 x BasicBlock(
          (conv1): Conv2d(32, 1, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn1): BatchNorm2d(1, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
          (conv2): Conv2d(1, 32, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn2): BatchNorm2d(32, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (layer4): Sequential(
    (0): PAIModulePyThread(
      (layerArray): ModuleList(
        (0-3): 4 x BasicBlock(
          (conv1): Conv2d(32, 1, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(2, 2), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn1): BatchNorm2d(1, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
          (conv2): Conv2d(1, 64, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn2): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (downsample): Sequential(
            (0): Conv2d(1, 64, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(2, 2), bias=False)
            (1): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          )
        )
      )
    )
    (1): PAIModulePyThread(
      (layerArray): ModuleList(
        (0-3): 4 x BasicBlock(
          (conv1): Conv2d(64, 1, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn1): BatchNorm2d(1, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
          (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)
          (conv2): Conv2d(1, 64, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), bias=False)
          (bn2): BatchNorm2d(64, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
        )
      )
    )
  )
  (avgpool): AdaptiveAvgPool2d(output_size=(1, 1))
  (fc): PAIModulePyThread(
    (layerArray): ModuleList(
      (0-3): 4 x Linear(in_features=64, out_features=1000, bias=True)
    )
  )
